<script>
(function(){
		/*
		  腾讯网适配跳转
		*/
		var reWriteUrl = function(url){
			if(url){
				if(url.indexOf("/a/")>0 ){
					var Splits = url.split("/"),siteName=Splits[2].split("qq.com")[0].split(".").length==3?siteName=Splits[2].split("qq.com")[0].split(".")[0]+"_"+Splits[2].split("qq.com")[0].split(".")[1]:siteName=Splits[2].split("qq.com")[0].split(".")[0],aids=url.split("/a/")[1].replace(/[^0-9]/g, ""),site="";
					if(typeof siteName!=="undefined" && typeof aids!=="undefined"){
						if(siteName.split(".").length>2){
							var len = siteName.split(".").length;
							for(var i=0;i<len;i++){
									site+=siteName.split(".")[i];
									if(i<len-2){
										site+="_";
									}
							}
						}else{
							site=siteName.split(".")[0];
						}
						return "http://xw.qq.com/c/"+siteName+"/"+aids;
					}
				}
			}
		};
		var goToMobile = function(){
				var Aarry = document.getElementsByTagName("a"),TmpArray=[];
				for(var i=0;i<Aarry.length;i++){
					TmpArray[i]=Aarry[i].href.toString();
					if(TmpArray[i].split("/")[3]=="a"){
						Aarry[i].href=reWriteUrl(TmpArray[i]);
					}
				}
				
		}
		var mobileSietList={news:"news",photo:"photo",video:"video",view:"huati",finance:"finance",ent:"ent",sports:"sports",digi:"digi",mil:"mil",lady:"lady",auto:"auto",games:"games",house:"house",astro:"astro",cul:"cul",fashion:"fashion","2014":"shijiebei"};
		
		if(/Android|webOS|iPhone|Windows Phone|iPod|BlackBerry|SymbianOS/i.test(navigator.userAgent)){
			/*底层页跳转*/
			var url=window.location.href;
			var pathname=window.location.pathname;
			if(url.indexOf("/a/")>0 && window.location.hostname!="www.nanjing2014.org"){
				if(url.indexOf("?pc")<0){
				try{
					window.location.href=reWriteUrl(url);
				}catch(e){}
				}
			}else{ // 频道首页跳转
				if(url.indexOf("?mobile")<0){
					var mobileUrl=window.location.hostname.split(".")[0];
					if(/news|pp|video|view|finance|ent|sports|digi|mil|fashion|auto|games|house|astro|cul|2014/i.test(mobileUrl)){
						try{
							window.location.href='http://xw.qq.com/m/'+mobileSietList[mobileUrl]+'/index.htm';
						}catch(e){	
						}
					}
				}
			}
			try{
				//document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', goToMobile, false);
			}catch(e){	
			}
		}
})();

</script><!--[if !IE]>|xGv00|90aa1684ef88dade8c69fde7463d9e36<![endif]-->

				UI.localData.set("loginTime", (new Date()).getTime())
			} catch(b) {}
		}
	},
	loginOut: function() {
		var a = (new Date).getTime();
		UI.cookie("skey", "", "", "", "qq.com");
		UI.cookie("uin", "", "", "", "qq.com");
		UI.cookie("luin", "", "", "", "qq.com");
		UI.cookie("lskey", "", "", "", "qq.com");

		UI.$("loginWrap").innerHTML = this.noLoginHtml
	},

				login.cbArr[a]()
			}
		}
		login.loginCheck();
		login.cbLogin();
		login.cleanCbLogin()
	},

	}

		function createHiddenInput(name, value, disabled) {
			if(elems[name]) {
				elems[name].value = value;
				if(disabled) elems[name].disabled = 'disabled';
				else elems[name].removeAttribute('disabled');
				return elems[name];
			}
			try{
				var element = document.createElement('<input name="'+name+'" />');
			}catch(e){}
			
			if(!element || element.nodeName.toUpperCase() != 'INPUT'){
				var element = document.createElement('input');		
			}
			element.type = 'hidden';
			element.name = name;
			element.value = value;
			if(disabled)
				element.disabled = disabled;
			frm.appendChild(element);
			return element;
		}

<script language="javascript">
function ShowDateFileBak()
{
    var myfm = $C("index_history");

    if(myfm.Channel.selectedIndex==0){ alert("请选择频道"); return false;}
    if(myfm.Year.value=="")   { alert("请选择年份"); return false;}
    if(myfm.Month.value=="")  { alert("请选择月份"); return false;}
    if(myfm.Day.value=="")    { alert("请选择日期"); return false;}
    if(myfm.Time.selectedIndex==0)   { alert("请选择时间"); return false;}
	
    channel = myfm.Channel.options[myfm.Channel.selectedIndex].value;
    year    = myfm.Year.value;
    month   = myfm.Month.value;
    day     = myfm.Day.value;
    time    = myfm.Time.options[myfm.Time.selectedIndex].value;

    if((year==2005 && month<10)||(year==2005 && month==10 && day<20) || year < 2005)
    {
        alert("各频道首页往日回顾是从2005年10月20日开始的");
		return false;
    }
	    
    if(channel == "stock")
    {
    	loadurl = "http://finance.qq.com/stock/b/history/index"+year+month+day+time+".shtml";
    }
    else
    {   
    	loadurl = "http://"+channel+".qq.com/b/history/index"+year+month+day+time+".shtml";
    }

   // controlWindow=window.open(loadurl,"_blank");
   $C("history_submit").action=loadurl;
   $C("history_submit").submit();
    return false;
}
</script>

				<script>
					function $C(objectId) {
				  if(document.getElementById && document.getElementById(objectId)) {
				// W3C DOM
				return document.getElementById(objectId);
				  } else if (document.all && document.all(objectId)) {
				// MSIE 4 DOM
				return document.all(objectId);
				  } else if (document.layers && document.layers[objectId]) {
				// NN 4 DOM.. note: this won't find nested layers
				return document.layers[objectId];
				  } else {
				return false;
				  }
				
				}
				var today = new Date();
				var  hours=today.getHours();
				var  minutes=today.getMinutes();
				var UrlS= location.href;
				var DtaId =location.href.split("/");

				function getFullYear(d)
					{
						yr=d.getYear();if(yr<1000)
						yr+=1900;return yr;
					}
				
					function JCalendar (year,month,date) {
					var _date = arguments.length == 0 ? new Date() : new Date(year,month-1,date);
					//实例变量
					this.year = _date.getFullYear();
					this.month = _date.getMonth() + 1;
					this.date = _date.getDate();
					this.fday = new Date(this.year,this.month-1,1).getDay();//每月第一天的前一天星期数
					this.dayNum = new Date(this.year,this.month,0).getDate();//每月的天数
					//成员变量，当前年月日
					JCalendar.cur_year = this.year;
					JCalendar.cur_month = this.month;
					JCalendar.cur_date = _date.getDate();
					setCurTime({F:$C("index_history"),Y:JCalendar.cur_year,M:JCalendar.cur_month,D:JCalendar.cur_date});
				}
				JCalendar.prototype.show = function(){
					var fday = new Date(this.year,this.month-1,1).getDay();//每月第一天的星期数
					//日历里的每个单元格的数据，预先定义一段空数组，对应日历里第一周空的位置。[注意星期天对应的数是0]
					var date = new Array(fday > 0 ? fday : 0);
					var dayNum = new Date(this.year,this.month,0).getDate();//每月的天数
					var html_str = new Array();//保存日历控件的HTML代码
					var date_index = 0;//date数组的索引
					var weekDay = ["一","二","三","四","五"];
					for(var j = 1; j <= this.dayNum; j++){//初始化date数组
						date.push(j);
					}
					html_str.push("<div id='selectYM'><span id='newPreY' class='selectDataBtn' role='button' title='上一年份' onclick=\"JCalendar.update(-12);return false\"></span><span id='newPreM' class='selectDataBtn' role='button' title='上一月份' onclick=\"JCalendar.update(-1);return false\"></span><p id='calendar_title'>" + this.year + "年" + this.month + "月</p><span id='newNextM' class='selectDataBtn' role='button' title='下一月份' onclick=\"JCalendar.update(1);return false\"></span><span id='newNextY' class='selectDataBtn' role='button' title='下一年份' onclick=\"JCalendar.update(12);return false\"></span></div>");
					html_str.push("<table id='calendar'>");
					html_str.push("<tr>");
					html_str.push("<td style='color:#CC0000;padding:0 0 4px'>日</td>");
					for(var i = 0; i < 5; i++){//填充日历头
						html_str.push("<td style='padding:0 0 4px'>" + weekDay[i] + "</td>");
					}
					html_str.push("<td  style='color:#008000;padding:0 0 4px'>六</td>");
					html_str.push("</tr>");
					//日历主体
					var tmp;
					for(var i = 0; i < 6; i++){//填充日期，6行7列
						html_str.push("<tr>");
						for(var j = 0; j < 7; j++){
							tmp = date[date_index++];
							tmp = tmp ? tmp : "";
							if(tmp == this.date)
								html_str.push("<td><div class='newDWrap' id='c_today'><div class='newDWrap' onclick='JCalendar.click(this)'>" + JCalendar.cur_date + "</div></div></td>");
							else if(tmp == "")
								html_str.push("<td></td>");
							else
								html_str.push("<td><div class='newDWrap' onclick='JCalendar.click(this)'>" + tmp + "</div></td>");
						}
						html_str.push("</tr>");
					}
					
					html_str.push("</table>");
					return html_str.join("");
				}
				//静态方法
				JCalendar.update = function(_month){
					var date = new Date(JCalendar.cur_year,JCalendar.cur_month - 1 + _month,1);
					var fday = date.getDay();//每月第一天的星期数
					var year = date.getFullYear();
					var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
					var dayNum = new Date(JCalendar.cur_year,JCalendar.cur_month  + _month,0).getDate();//每月的天数
					var tds = document.getElementById("calendar").getElementsByTagName("td");
					for(var i = 7; i < tds.length; i++)//清空日历内容
						tds[i].innerHTML = "";
					document.getElementById("calendar_title").innerHTML = year + "年" + month + "月";//更新显示年月
					//更新当前年月
					JCalendar.cur_year = year;
					JCalendar.cur_month = month;
					for(var j = 1; j <= dayNum; j++){
						if(j == JCalendar.cur_date)
							tds[6 + fday + j].innerHTML = "<div id='c_today'><div class='newDWrap' onclick='JCalendar.click(this)'>" + JCalendar.cur_date + "</div></div>";
						else
							tds[6 + fday + j].innerHTML = "<div class='newDWrap' onclick='JCalendar.click(this)'>" + j + "</div>";
					}
					JCalendar.onupdate(year,month,JCalendar.cur_date);
				}
				
				JCalendar.onupdate = function(year,month,date){//日历更改时执行的函数，可以更改为自己需要函数,控件传递过来的参数为当前日期
					//alert(year + "年" + month + "月" + date + "日");
				}
				
				JCalendar.click = function(obj){
					
					var newOAllTableDiv = document.getElementById('calendar').getElementsByTagName('div');	
					for(var i=0,len = newOAllTableDiv.length;i<len;i++){
							//console.log(newOAllTableDiv[i].parentNode.tagName)
							if(newOAllTableDiv[i].parentNode.tagName.toLowerCase() == 'td'){
								newOAllTableDiv[i].className = 'newDWrap';
								}
						}
					obj.className = 'newDWrap newSelectThis';
					var tmp = document.getElementById("c_today");
					
					//tmp.innerHTML = "<div class='newDWrap' onmouseover=\"this.className='newDWrap'\" onmouseout=\"this.className='newDWrap'\" onclick='JCalendar.click(this)'>" + tmp.innerHTML + "</div>";
				
					JCalendar.cur_date = parseInt(obj.innerHTML);
					obj.innerHTML =  obj.innerHTML ;
					JCalendar.onclick(JCalendar.cur_year,JCalendar.cur_month,JCalendar.cur_date);
				
				}
				
				/**/
				JCalendar.onclick = function (year,month,date){
						//alert(today.getYear())

						var mo =today.getMonth()+1; 
						if(month.toString().length==1){
							month = "0"+month.toString();
						}
						if(date.toString().length==1){
							date = "0"+date.toString();
						}
						var ty=year.toString();
						var tm=month.toString();
						var td=date.toString();
						var url;
						switch(true){
							case year >getFullYear(today):
								ty=getFullYear(today);tm=mo;td=today.getDate();
								alert("今天才"+getFullYear(today)+"年"+mo+"月"+today.getDate()+"号哦~");
								break;
							case (year==getFullYear(today))&&(month>mo):
								ty=getFullYear(today);tm=mo;td=today.getDate();
								alert("今天才"+getFullYear(today)+"年"+mo+"月"+today.getDate()+"号哦~");

							case (year==getFullYear(today))&&(month==mo)&&(date>today.getDate()):

							case (year ==getFullYear(today))&&(month==mo)&&(date==today.getDate()):

								alert("您正在查看这个页面！");
								break;
							case isNaN(year):case isNaN(month):case isNaN(date):break;
						}
						setCurTime({F:$C("index_history"),Y:ty,M:tm,D:td})
				
				}
				function setCurTime(a){
						if(typeof a != "object")	return;
						a.M=a.M.toString();
						a.D=a.D.toString();
						if(a.M.length==1){
							a.M = "0"+a.M;
						}
						if(a.D.length==1){
							a.D = "0"+a.D;
						}
						var f=a.F;
						setSelected(f.Year,a.Y);
						setSelected(f.Month,a.M);
						setSelected(f.Day,a.D);		$C("selected_date").innerHTML=a.Y+"-"+(a.M.length==1?"0"+a.M:a.M)+"-"+(a.D.length==1?"0"+a.D:a.D);
					}
					//alert("0"+parseInt("02").toString())
					function setSelected(a,b){//a:select obj,b:value index_history
						if(!a || typeof a != "object")	return;
						if(!b)	return;
						a.value=b;
						/*
						var l=a.options.length;
						for(var i=0;i<l;i++){
							if(a.options[i].value == b){
								a.options[i].selected = true;
							}
						}
						*/
					}
				function opens(){
				$C('rili').style.display='block';
				}
				function cloese(){
				$C('rili').style.display='none';
				}
				  document.getElementById("calendar_contain").innerHTML = new JCalendar().show();
				</script>

function bossZoneHandler()
{
    var sFlag=false;
	this.registerZone2 = function (ev,clickType)
	{
	    var loopTryNum = 10;
	    var bossID = 1337; 
		  
	    try
		{		
		    //qq
			var a=document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^|)o_cookie=([^;]*)(;|$)'));
			var iQQ=(a==null?"":unescape(a[2]));
			var purl='';
			var zoneId='';
			
			if(typeof clickType == 'undefined')
			{
			    if(sFlag) return true;
		        var ev = window.event || ev;
		        var et = ev.srcElement || ev.target;
			    var type=et.tagName;
		        if (type != "A" && type != "IMG" ) 
			    {
			        return true;
			    } 
			
			    if (type == "A")
			    {
			        purl = et.href;
			    }
			    else if (type == "IMG")
			    {
			        purl = et.parentNode.href;
			    }
			
			    //pseudo attr
			    for (var i=loopTryNum-1,tagNode=et;i>=0;i--,tagNode=tagNode.parentNode)
			    {
			        if(tagNode.attributes['bossZone'])
				    {
			            zoneId = tagNode.attributes['bossZone'].nodeValue;
				    } else if(tagNode.attributes['bosszone'])
				    {
				        zoneId = tagNode.attributes['bosszone'].nodeValue;
				    }
				    else if(tagNode.attributes['BossZone'])
				    {
				        zoneId = tagNode.attributes['BossZone'].nodeValue;
				    }
				    else if(tagNode.attributes['Bosszone'])
				    {
				        zoneId = tagNode.attributes['Bosszone'].nodeValue;
				    }

			        if(zoneId) break; 
			    }		
			    if(!zoneId) return;
			}
			else
			{
			    zoneId = ev.bossZone;
				purl = ev.url;
				sFlag = true;
				setTimeout(function (){sFlag = false;},200);
			}
			
			var localUrl = location.href;
			var site = localUrl.substring(7,localUrl.indexOf('.qq.com'));
			site = site.substr(site.lastIndexOf('.')+1);

			var iurl = 'http://btrace.qq.com/collect?sIp=&iQQ='+iQQ+'&sBiz=qq.com&sOp='+zoneId+'&iSta=&iTy='+bossID+'&iFlow=&sSite='+site+'&sUrl='+escape(purl)+'&sLocalUrl='+escape(location.href)+'&'+Math.random();
			gImage = new Image(1,1);
			gImage.src = iurl;
		} catch (e) {}
	}

function hideGoTop(){
    var scrollTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop + document.body.scrollTop;
    document.getElementById("goTop").style.display = scrollTop > 400 ? "block" : "none";
    document.getElementById("wxsys").style.display = scrollTop > 400 ? "block" : "none";
    document.getElementById("wxsys").onmouseover = function(){
    	document.getElementById("erweima").style.display = "block";
    }
    document.getElementById("wxsys").onmouseout = function(){
    	document.getElementById("erweima").style.display = "none";
    }
}
window.onscroll = function(){
    hideGoTop();
}

			$(".shishipai").hide();
			$(".shishipai_bg").hide();
		})
	})
	$(".branding h1").bind("click",function(){
		$(".shishipai").animate({opacity:"1"}).show();
		$(".shishipai_bg").css({"height":$("body").height()}).show();
		if ($.browser.msie && ($.browser.version == "6.0") && !$.support.style) { 
			$(".shishipai").css({"position":"absolute","top":$(document).scrollTop()+201})
		} 
		shishipaiTimer();
	})
	
	function shishipaiTimer(){
		shishipai.index=0;
		clearInterval(shishipai.timer);
		shishipai.timer = setInterval(function(){
			shishipai.index++;
			if(shishipai.index==6){
				$(".shishipai").animate({opacity:"0"},function(){
			$(".shishipai").hide();
			$(".shishipai_bg").hide();
		});
				clearInterval(shishipai.timer);
			}
		},1000)
	}
	
	$(window).scroll(function() {
		if ($.browser.msie && ($.browser.version == "6.0") && !$.support.style) { 
			$(".shishipai").css({"top":$(document).scrollTop()+201})
		} 
		
	});
	
})()

(function(){

	var s_url = 'http://news.qq.com';
	var ua = navigator.userAgent;
	var r = new Date().getTime();

	var yytOffsetTop = $('#yyt').offset().top;
	if(isTTK){

		});
	}

			curIndex = 0;

		}

			curIndex = 1;
